Mr. Sun Myung Moon's Selected Words
73
Mr. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon Jo

1)
Prayer
Good morning! Is everyone here just family members? "Yes." Are the trainees here as well? Did the trainees attend? "No." So there are none, right? As you all know, this is the Barrytown training center. The reason you have gathered here is to fulfill the significant mission of how to connect the fate of America, which represents the democratic world of this era, with God's will in the future. I believe you take pride in being gathered here like this. One thing I want to know is how many American Jews are here—please raise your hands. Count them. About 50. Next, how about German Americans? "About 150." Then British Americans must be the majority. How many British Americans are there? "About 250." Next, how about Japanese Americans? Ah, I see.

Purpose of Fasting Prayer
Now, I believe you have resolved to fast for three days starting tomorrow in Washington. I know there are new family members here, or perhaps some who are seeing the teacher for the first time, and I would like those who are fasting for the first time and those seeing the teacher for the first time to raise their hands. Everyone except those seeing the teacher for the first time can lower their hands. I expect that those of you seeing the teacher for the first time will think, "The teacher looks very much like this." (Laughter) These days, on July 21, 1974, at the Barrytown training center (New York, USA).

8   Prayer
I've been traveling a lot by the sea, so my face is tanned black. So you might think the teacher is Asian but looks like a black person, but please don't think that way. (Laughter) Now, that was a joke. (Laughter, applause) The majority of the audience gathered here are spirited young people. You all have different nationalities and positions, but you are prepared to appear as one for a single purpose. The fact that nearly 600 people have gathered in one place to engage in a three-day fasting prayer is something we take pride in as a historical event.

Why must we do such a thing? We know that fasting is not a normal activity. Even if you skip lunch for one day, you naturally worry and think it’s a big deal. If someone is sick and has to fast for a day, that individual and their entire family will be concerned. If you don’t eat for three days, you might think you will die. You tend to think you will die. (Laughter) Even if it happens naturally, it is a worrying event, but the fact that we voluntarily decided to fast for three days is something remarkable and commendable.

Those of you who have fasted know that fasting is not that easy. However, to become a formal member of our Unification Church, one must fast for a week. You know that those who do not do so cannot become formal members. Generally, people believe that if they go without food for a week or eight days, they will die.

Why do we do this? It is an event of our church to confirm that we are centered on a purpose that risks our lives. We do this for whom? We do it for God. And for whom else? We do it for humanity. And for whom else do we do this? We do this to defend against Satan. We fast with the firm belief that this is a defensive line against Satan. Also, for us as individuals, by engaging in such fasting, we can always eliminate the fear of life. We fast to gain this confidence.

Having the conviction that "even if I fast for a week, I will advance for a single purpose and a global will" becomes the greatest tradition. If there is someone who has the conviction to fight for the purpose without dying even while continuing this week-long fast, that person is someone who cannot be surpassed by any religion or any representative of any religious community in the world, regardless of ethnic ideology.

Our starting point is not for the happiness of any individual but is a determined march to fulfill God's will in this world. This determination will remain the same for youth, the elderly, or those at the end of their lives. Because we have established a historical tradition through this fasting, the fact that we are engaging in a fasting struggle based on our current position in America is more terrifying than any demonstration or military action.

Prayer should not be for me but for the world. You all have fasted for a week, so I believe there is no problem in fasting for another week. What if we decide to fast for two weeks? I believe everyone here will participate in a two-week fast. What if we fast for three weeks? I believe you will all participate in that as well. Is that possible? "Yes." (Applause)

If such a number fasts for three weeks for the nation and the world, it cannot be anything but a global event. All medical professionals and many nations will focus their attention on this global major event. (Laughter) When looking at history, this will be a more astonishing event than any war or major event in the historical era and will become a driving force that can move history.

If you ask someone, "Would you prefer to die or fast for three weeks?" they would likely respond, "Well, if I’m going to die while fasting anyway, I’d rather die." (Laughter) Why? Because they would think they are bound to die during the fast anyway, during a three-week fast... (Laughter, applause)

However, for us, there is no problem. You can think of fasting for three days as similar to not sleeping for one night or skipping one meal. You should have this mindset and think, "This is a practice of fasting struggle." With that understanding, you should not be afraid or think it’s strange; rather, you should naturally do everything you need to do and sing while passing through these three days normally.

When fasting, your face should not look shabby. You should put on makeup and apply color, and do everything. Women should wear beautiful clothes. (Laughter) When you fast, many people will come to watch. (Laughter) When they see you, they might think, "Oh, look at them fasting..." (Making a funny expression) (Laughter) If you look all droopy like this... (Laughter) Those who are meaningful participants in this fast will be observing. "Ah, these people are starting their fast so vigorously." They might not think they are watching, but there will be people watching. "What will it be like at the end? They will be eager to eat." Many will think in various ways. Therefore, I hope you remain calm and composed at both the beginning and the end.

Those of you who have fasted for seven days will feel how serious the last five minutes before midnight on the last day is. You will think, "Once these five minutes pass, I will start eating." Once those five minutes pass, it will be a new day, and on the first moment of the eighth day, you must not think about "food." Even if it’s just for ten minutes, you must clear your mind for at least ten minutes. You must think that what we pray for is not for me but for the world. You must not think about food first. Only then will it rise; otherwise, it will go down. Therefore, when you fast for three days, you should have the determination to fast for four days. It should always be like that. So I hope you will definitely make that determination and return accordingly. Will you do that? "Yes."

The Christian Spirit in God's Providence and America's Mission
Now let’s talk about it. As you know, America is the leading country of the democratic world. God has looked upon this world and has nurtured democracy because He loves it. Since America is the country representing the democratic world, God has raised it to become a leading nation in the world. It is not that the American people are great that this has happened; it has come about to fulfill God's will within His providence. Therefore, God's will is for America to develop alongside Him, which is the original spirit that formed America.

From that perspective, when we look at present-day America, it is difficult to see that America fully embodies the image of a nation where God can truly reside and where it can lead the world with God's love and will. It is an obvious conclusion that if there were no God and Christianity, America and its people could not have been formed.

You know that the American people are a mixed ethnicity. Yet, who has taken on the responsibility to connect this? It is Christianity that has done so. Therefore, America has been centered around Christianity, sharing the same cultural sphere and way of life. We cannot deny that having the same purpose and way of life has become the motive for unity. Because the spiritual and practical foundations centered on Christianity and all traditions were the same, they could unite both internally and externally. You see, the way of life of Western people generally involves eating bread and having similar living conditions. This is because, due to Christian thought, a deep connection has been formed even in the most profound aspects of life.

Today, that has taken shape as a national representative form, resulting in a comprehensive national identity in America. Based on that, the development of the church and economic progress began to occur in tandem. In other words, it is believed that the motivation for America's economic development has been centered around public purposes and a unified Christian advancement among well-believing believers.

America was originally formed as a nation that fled from Europe, having been expelled and persecuted, so you should understand that the conviction of not being inferior to Europe was prevalent among your ancestors. The American people stood as a group persecuted and rejected by Europe, and they had to have a strong internal bond to unite powerfully, which is a fact that could not be avoided. Thus, America has been developing a new Christian culture at a higher level while engaging in the act of uniting well-believing Europeans and well-believing Christians. By doing so, they have been able to absorb those who genuinely wish to live centered around Christian faith in Europe, which has become a motive for America to unite not only Europeans but also prominent intellectuals from around the world.

How was this possible? Why was it possible? It was because there was Christianity. In other words, there could not be any remarkable individual or any nation capable of absorbing this vast Christian cultural sphere, and the founding leaders of America and the subsequent American people understood this. Therefore, we cannot deny that Christianity is the foundational spirit of America's founding ideology and has become its traditional spirit.

If this Christian spirit had developed further, becoming more progressive and advancing in a direction that serves the world, America would have had a significant mission in globalizing God's will alongside Christianity. Then God would have made the world one centered around America, and America would have fulfilled its mission as the only nation in saving the world. This is how we see it.

The Greatest Power in America is the Christian Spirit
13
If the day comes when the Christian spirit in America is broken, you must understand that America will become a country that is easier to disintegrate and fall apart than any other nation. And if all economic trends lead to the current miserable state of the world, America will become a form that cannot be salvaged by anyone.

Why? Because at that time, people will unite only among their own ethnic groups. They will start to think about their own ethnicity. Jews will think only of Jews. Germans will think only of Germans. This will lead to competition and conflict among the different ethnic groups within the country. If such possibilities arise, America will be seen as broken.

The greatest power in America is the Christian spirit. It is the very fact that America has achieved a super-ethnic union through the Christian spirit that constitutes America's greatness. And because the social organization and economic system centered on Christian thought have been emphasized until now, America is considered great. The direction of policies, guided by God's will, and the perspective of what America will do in front of the world all stem from God and Christian thought, which cannot be denied.

This America, formed in this way—this America blessed by God—has made progressive advancements while inheriting God's will, yet you are now at a stage where you can feel that it is not in a stage of development but is moving toward a crisis state.

As you know, today when it comes to Christianity, young people shake their heads. You are also well aware that many clergy who would dedicate their lives to Christianity are now deviating. No matter how much the youth oppose, if there are leaders and a leadership system within Christianity that can unite more powerfully than the opposing youth, there is hope that at any time, we can restore a nation and its future. However, the Christian leaders who should take on that subjective mission are...
The fact that we are in a state of decline is an indication of the results of both internal and external failure. 

When viewed this way, hope for the church has reached a state of despair. Moreover, if you look at your families, family ethics have fundamentally collapsed as well. This collapse has brought about results akin to a radical infiltration of America by a demonic force, coinciding with the downfall of Christian thought. A nation that cannot establish a standard of trust in the state and cannot set a reliable basis for family is left wondering what it can believe in. What can it rely on?

We know well that America is at a stage where individualism is bearing fruit. When asked, "Is there a family?" they respond, "There is no family relationship. It’s all about me." In contrast, when asked, "Is there a country? Will you take responsibility for the country?" they say, "What is a country? We don’t know." 

So, who is the owner of this country? Is it the individualists? A nation should be able to guide individualists, but we are at a stage where there is no relationship between the state, individualists, and you. Such a nation will go its own way, and families will flow in their own direction. Individualistic individuals may remain, but you must understand that the families you belong to and your nation will flow away and perish.

For the sake of God's will and the destiny of Christianity, should we just leave America, a nation standing in crisis, as it is? If we realize that America, when properly managed, has the potential to bring the world under its control, then we cannot help but acknowledge that America’s enemies will be more interested in eroding this nation than anyone else. Because the American people are in a personal position, they all refuse to take up arms and fight for their country when it comes to life and death issues. The day will come when the powerful ideology that surpasses the individualism held by the American people will manifest in a collective form, and America will have to surrender before us. What kind of nation is that? It is the Communist Party, your enemy. The Communist Party is not only the enemy of America and the democratic world but also the enemy of God. It is the enemy of God.

So, who will defend against this? This is the responsibility of Christianity. Yet, Christianity is in a state of decline. This nation, which was established to represent Christianity and fulfill God's will, lacks the ability to do so. This is not only a crisis for America but also a crisis for the democratic world, and it is a providential crisis centered on God. Isn't this a reasonable conclusion?

Then, who will defend against this? We cannot rely on the Christianity present in America today. It is obvious that even the believers of Christianity today cannot handle this, nor can the power of any organization of young people who believe in Christianity. Therefore, focusing on the state of decline of such Christianity, we have reached a stage where we need to regroup the foundation of Christianity and establish a strong new Christian movement or church movement with powerful new theories. However, it seems that we are the only ones capable of doing this within America.

What has been evidenced through this conference is that no religious organization can gather 200 young people to engage in a hunger strike together. This conclusion has been reached. It has been determined that only Reverend Moon's organization can do this. Therefore, a request came from the White House to mobilize 200 members. 

What does this say? It indicates that when America is in crisis, there are no young people willing to risk their lives and stand at the forefront. From this perspective, you must realize that we have a historical mission. We have raised this banner not for the Unification Church but for the revival of God's will and the spirit of Christianity. Therefore, we must understand the responsibility we have taken on. In this light, we must recognize how much God trusts us and how much He can only look to us with all His hopes.

Moreover, this is a great opportunity for our enemies, who wish for Christianity to perish, to realize that Christianity can be revived through us. When they understand that through us, the light can be rekindled for Christianity to rise again, how fearful will they be of us?

Thus, the democratic world can be reborn, and the hopes of your ancestors, who shed blood to establish this nation, can unfold into a new dimension. The path for your descendants to follow the providence of heaven without wandering will be opened. When we think of these facts, we must recognize that we have taken on a historical mission. From this perspective, you should head to Washington with pride. Isn't this a great opportunity to represent all of America and occupy the city of Washington from a providential standpoint?

You must understand that the enemy of America lies within the internal citizens and families. There are two paths to a nation's downfall: one through external forces and the other through internal corruption. You know that Rome fell not due to external attacks but because of internal corruption. When we look at all the external standards of America today, the stage for downfall due to external attacks has not yet arrived. Now, where is America's enemy? It is not in the external world but in the internal world. You must understand that it lies within your citizens and your families. This stems from the collapse of Christian faith and the collapse of family ethics.

History shows that whenever the issue of ethics collapses in any nation, that nation inevitably falls. Among your societal trends, there is a tendency to change wives and live with different partners. You must recognize that this is the underlying flow of America that you do not know about. 

People are loving for the sake of their own enjoyment, doing whatever they please. They act according to their own desires, enjoying anything they like even in public. Young intellectuals in America, who should be taking on the significant responsibility of the future and present of America, are now causing problems on college campuses by engaging in streaking. 

Can such groups find ideal families or exemplary ethics based on Christian thought? No, they cannot. Desire only leads to chaos, confusion, and despair. Until now, young people have engaged in such acts to stimulate something new in history, but now there is nothing left to stimulate them. They may run alone, but soon men will carry women, and women will carry men in their games. What will happen next? Eventually, they will not only run but also say, "Let’s do whatever we want," embracing each other and dancing in the courtyard. This will ruin the universities and the nation.

Those who do not feel satisfied with this need new stimulation. They will say to the old-fashioned people who oppose them, "We have wrapped everything up. Let it all go. We will do whatever we want, the youth of this era. What you oppose is what we love the most." They will declare, "What the old-fashioned people like is what we hate the most, and what they dislike is what we love the most." They need stimulation, but what could be a greater stimulation than this? Initially, there will only be riots, riots that kill people and spill blood. 

When it reaches that stage, if any young person claims, "Communism is the best for us," they will all flock to it at once. Riots can happen all at once. There is a danger that young people could turn to communism in an instant.

If that happens, how will you stop it? Can you mobilize America's military power to stop it? I know that the Communist Party is working on internal groundwork in this direction. The Communist Party seeks to corrupt those who do not want to work or engage in collective actions through drugs. For those who do not want to be interfered with... When that day comes, the Communist Party will be able to operate without touching America. If the American people were to turn to communism, do you think the Communist Party would love and care for all American citizens? They would become the princes of exploitation in the world, a lineage of exploiters. Therefore, they will persecute.

From this perspective, what guarantees that America will not end up like this in the future? There is none. The majority opinion is that it cannot be prevented, and that is the prevailing sentiment. Then, does God want it to turn out this way? It is astonishing that America, centered on Christian thought, has become so individualistic. This is because Christianity has not taken responsibility, and the leaders of Christianity have failed in their duties.

To protect America, the Unification Church must mobilize everything at the right time. God cannot leave the leaders of Christianity behind. If there are such Christians and leaders of Christianity, God will desire a new denomination that advocates for His will and calls forth those who assert His will. From that perspective, we, the Unification Church, have raised the banner. Christianity, which has failed to take responsibility for the nation and the people, must fulfill its duties in protecting the nation and the citizens, yet it is wholeheartedly opposing the Unification Church, which seeks to protect a new Christianity and the nation.

We must recognize that we exist as a great force united for the sake of America, the whole world, and God's will. Those who are concerned about God's will and the future of America will undoubtedly be watching us with interest.

From this perspective, what does the Unification Church possess? It has a philosophical tradition that can unify Christianity. You all know this well without me having to say it. Do you know? "Yes." We are aware that we can develop this nation and this people to reach the depths of God's heart that have not yet been achieved. It is decisive that we can develop to a higher dimension. Therefore, we must take pride in the fact that we are not only preventing the collapse of the historical Christian thought in America but also paving the way to a higher dimension. You must surely understand that this is the case. Do you understand? "Yes."

But what is the problem? The problem is time. There is no time. If we were given 10 or 50 years, there would be no problem, but the historical situation and the global situation do not allow for such time. If we do not accomplish this within 4 or 6 years, everything will go wrong.

That is why what I presented to you is that from 1977 to 1978, we prepared for these issues, and unless we lay the foundation for all of America, we cannot protect and defend America. The question is, who will be the group capable of doing this? We have understood the will, we have such influence within ourselves, and we have certainly set our path, so we must recognize that we should automatically resolve to invest all sacrifices at this time.

Then, who should do this work? It is not someone else. It is us. We must do it. Among us, who should do it? I believe it should be the young people. If the citizens of America, blessed by heaven, are to take on the leading responsibility for this nation and the democratic world, then we, who understand that will, must naturally take responsibility.

The Unification Church serves as a bulwark to defend a failing America. 

When you think about this, it is strange. The person asking you to fast is Mr. Moon from Korea, who came from the East. Can this be possible? Without God's will and Christianity, it is impossible. If I were not connected to such traditional thought, I would also wish for America to fail. The American people do not just do well wherever they go. I am someone who knows all the ailments and flaws. However, I know that God's will must not depart from here, which is why I am doing this. I am doing this for God. The group gathered here is made up of young people.

Despite the numerous religious leaders and religious people in America, they cannot mobilize the citizens or the youth to do such things, so how is it that only the Unification Church can? This is because God is working with the Unification Church more than anyone else, and the Unification Church believes in and knows God's will more strongly than anyone else. This is a conclusion that can be drawn.

Thus, Mr. Moon will be able to gather the youth of the world. The fact that he has gathered American youth, who have fallen into a decadent state and cannot find their way, serves as evidence that he can gather the youth of the entire world. Is that not true? "Yes."

When we see such things, the results may not be immediately visible before our eyes, but when we consider history and tradition, we become confident that great achievements are being established here. We are not only defending the collapse of Christian thought in America but also take pride in having a progressive ideology. This nation will soon urgently demand such groups. This will not be done by a single denomination but by the nation sovereignly... Knowing this, we must take action.

We must understand that this will serve as a bulwark against the most terrifying forces that could lead to America's downfall. Moreover, since the current family ethics could ruin America, we are determined to establish new families and create a new national ethics among the American people. Do you see that as possible? "Yes." The "yes" that you young people have spoken is not a random statement. It is a decisive statement. We must become a group that stands up to defend against our families becoming enemies of heaven and falling into the hands of Satan.

We must recognize that we will not be absorbed into the strategies of Satan and the devil that undermine God's will and the future of heaven.

Therefore, our Unification Church must prepare for this by arming ourselves with the spirit of victory.
We are doing this externally. From that perspective, America will be saved spiritually because of us. Politically, it will defend against the threat of communism because of us. Then, the question remains: how will we address the economic issues? We can defend against the threat of communism, we can defend against the decline of Christianity, and we can defend against the decline of youth ethics. However, when it comes to the question of how to handle economic issues afterward, we are still not on a global trajectory. We cannot leave out communism. You surely know this from that perspective. You all have the belief that "because of us, America will change into a new America, will be established as a new America, and will be able to create a new world." Is that right? "Yes."

Without an economic foundation, we cannot lead the world. 

So, how will we handle economic issues in the future? This is a matter for the teacher. It cannot be a matter of leadership alone. While we can completely defend against internal issues, how will we handle external economic issues? We cannot lead the world without creating a system that can move America and the world centered on the economic power of our Unification Church. Therefore, you must understand that the teacher believes we must devise strong new methods in those areas and train accordingly.

We do not have factories in America, nor do we have any economic sponsors. We are like the naked. If we have nothing to wear, we must grow cotton and train ourselves to make clothing from that fiber. We must become refined individuals who can overcome the cold and heat.

To save this country and this world, vast economic power is needed. If we say we will take responsibility for this, we must be prepared to make any sacrifice to create the driving force that can support and move this forward. At that extreme point, we can study from various angles how to build the economic power necessary to move the Unification Church in America and develop it globally. This economic activity of yours... We must engage in a movement where each of us takes responsibility in this reality of life.

In recent years, I have heard that we are in an urgent stage where we must focus more on economic issues than on spiritual issues. The fact that you are fasting for three days is for the nation, the world, and God, but we must also resolve to endure not eating or wearing anything for the sake of the Unification Church in the future. We need time. We cannot find that time by being like others. We cannot act as if we are taking a break like others. Today, fasting and such training are also seen as helpful in preparing vast economic power for ourselves in the future.

Imagine if the Unification Church had a million members. If each of us donated $1 for the cause, that would amount to a million dollars. And if our million members fast for a week, how much would that be? Think about it. If the average salary in America is $700, then a quarter of that is $180. So how much would that be? It would be an astronomical amount. (Laughter) You would laugh. You would laugh.

If we use that money to build educational centers and support some government in the world, those who spend that money cannot help but think of this ideology. The teacher cannot help but think of such things. Why? It is not because I need money. I have some money for myself. However, I cannot earn money that can support America. So, I must earn money that can sustain us within America. Because we must definitely achieve this, the teacher feels a historical responsibility to train these young people to ensure they can accomplish this.

Therefore, the teacher believes that we must train American youth to earn $3,000 a month in the future. I am praying before heaven for that to happen. Without such radical training, we cannot lay the economic foundation necessary to bear this vast historical responsibility. If we do not do this, Unification Church members will have to suffer throughout their lives, struggling until they grow old and die. Will it be ten years of suffering? Twenty years of suffering? If given a choice, the teacher cannot help but think of making them suffer for ten or twenty years. (Laughter) So what path will you choose? Eat like pigs and work like oxen. Would you welcome that? "Yes." I have seen many American youths carrying their belongings.

Plans for the fishing industry and leaving a tradition for catching fish.

Everyone, for the past month or two, I have been going out to sea every day. You might think, "The teacher likes boats and the sea, so he goes." However, what I hope to do is to leave a tradition that the teacher does what anyone else cannot do. There is nothing else. (Laughter, applause)

Was it the day before yesterday? The day before yesterday, the wind was strong. When I went to the dock, there was a red flag saying, "Today is a dangerous day; do not go out to sea." The boat owner said, "It’s quite windy today; it would be better not to go out." "Oh, is that so? I understand." Then I went out early in the morning to catch fish. I know well that fishing does not work on windy days. When the wind blows, the fish do not bite. So I wandered around all day. Around two o'clock, I caught one bluefish.

The people there were saying, "Will this even be caught?" But when I caught the fish, I sent it back to the sea, saying, "Hey, go well." Then I said, "Since it’s windy today, let’s stop and fish on a calm day." After that, I went out with a small boat and caught seven flounders.

I know that my mother really likes that fish. (Laughter, applause) Since I was told to catch fish like flounder instead of bluefish or tuna, I thought that since I caught this impressive fish today, I should give it to my mother. But then I thought it would be better to give it to someone else, so I gave it to another person. (Laughter) I released one fish and gave another away, so we could take the rest home.

Then in the evening, around six o'clock, I came back and, despite the wind, went out again on a big boat. I took Mr. Choi and Mr. Yang, who came from Korea, saying, "Hey, let’s go today." As evening approached, I noticed that they were thinking it would be better not to go out since it was getting dark, but the instructors Choi and Yang from this training center said they had not caught any fish today, so I took them out again. We went out and caught forty-two bluefish. (Applause)

I knew you would come here today. I am here today, so you would surely come here, but you are fasting this morning. So I did not tell you to give all the fish to you, but I told you to let the trainees eat well. I instructed that only the trainees should share the fish. (Applause) I feel sorry for you who came to Belvedere and Barrytown, fasting and not even being able to eat breakfast, thinking about fasting again. (Laughter) I thought about that and had this idea. In fact, my heart aches. So what did I think? I thought that when you finish fasting in Washington, I should not just send you off but should ask you to come back here. (Applause) Do you want that? "Yes."

However, to feed these five or six hundred people, who will catch all the fish? (Laughter) Who will catch it? Would it be nice if the teacher caught it for you? "Yes." (Applause) If you fast for three days, even if you eat breakfast in Washington, you can eat that meal conditionally, and even if the teacher catches one fish, I promise to find a way to multiply it six hundred times for you. While you are fasting, I will mobilize boats to engage in fish-catching activities. (Applause)

When you finish your three-day fast and come here, I will not just send you off. If possible, I plan to add about three more days and give you some training before sending you off. (Applause) The costs will be directed to Mr. Kamiyama in New York to solve everything. (Laughter) So I will draw lots and take a few people with me on the boat. (Applause) When I take them, I will try to take those whom God loves and who are cherished by God. Such people will be the ones who win the lottery. They will be those who put in sincere effort. So you should know that and put in your sincere effort.

The reason I go out to sea on a boat is to establish a tradition. I love the sea. I love boats. So what do I want to do? I want to engage in a global fishing industry. Let’s Keep the Moment
I apologize for having you all gather here at the Belvedere Holy Ground, sitting in such a damp place. However, I hope you can sit here with a grateful heart for the clear weather that has come after the moon and the rainy days until yesterday. 
The title I would like to think about with you today is “Let’s Keep the Moment.” I will share a few words on this topic. 

The Moment in History and the Hope of Humanity
Here, you are all in your 20s or 30s, but that is also a moment in time. That is why we go through our childhood, youth, adulthood, and eventually reach old age. The passing of time in our lives is what we call the affairs of life. In this way, that moment is formed by connecting the moments of childhood, youth, and adulthood.

When we look at moments, there are times that are flat like plains, high times like mountains, and deep times like valleys. Let's Cross the Boundary Line 

The title of this morning's message is "Let's Cross the Boundary Line." Do you understand what that means? "Yes." We know that there is a boundary line in any realm or place. If you wake up early in the morning... Considering the time spent sleeping, there is a boundary line even in that sleeping time. There is a boundary line that says how many hours you can sleep without dozing off and how many hours you can go without sleeping. Sitting here is the same. There is a boundary line regarding how many hours you can sit. A day itself has a boundary point of 24 hours. 

Even in the principles of creation and the providence of restoration, there are boundary lines. 

When we look at the world of principles, we know that even the principle of creation itself is formed around a boundary point. We can understand that transcending this boundary point cannot be done solely by one's own power. Whether one receives a great stimulus or a great impulse of power, without such an action, one cannot cross this boundary line; this is something we can understand very logically. 

We must quickly cross the negative boundary lines, and we must expand the positive boundary lines. This is something we think about in our daily lives. One World 

We know that the world we live in has not become one world. We also know that this world is in competition among various countries. Everyone thinks and strives to make the world one centered around a particular country, or if it's their own country, centered around their own country. 

Everyone wants to create one centered around themselves. 

Looking at one country, even within one country, if there is a specific group or a specific ethnicity, it is customary to think of that group or ethnicity as the center and try to unify the country. When looking at any group or ethnicity, it is also the case that if there is a specific family, that family will try to unify the ethnicity or group. 

When looking at a family, in your own family, if you are yourself, you center around yourself; if you are a father, you center around your father; if you are a mother, you center around your mother; if you are a child, you center around your child. Each person wants to create one centered around themselves. 

Now, when we see that we all share this common idea, we can see that this has been a tradition passed down by countless ancestors who have come and gone, just as it is for us today. Regardless of the cultural development or the revolutionary processes that have occurred, we can infer that such traditional ideas have continued unchanged until today. 

Even when we live our lives in a position where the East and West cannot meet, we understand that the traditions of the East and West cannot deviate from this principle. 

The desire of humans is to create an environment and return to God. 

So, when we see this, the principle that one asserts oneself within their country, within their ethnicity, within their family, and within themselves, where does it start? If we look at it in reverse, an individual must create a family, a family must create an ethnicity, an ethnicity must create a nation, and a nation must create a world. If not, one cannot seek a unified world; therefore, this tradition must be established, and this theory is a valid conclusion. 

Now, our human desire... you all have desires. If we ask where those desires go, we can conclude that desires cannot go anywhere without going through such stages. 

Then, when we look at a man, what is the man's desire? A man does not only have desires for himself but also has desires for his family. Then, what is the desire of the family? It is to create an environment centered around the family. Once a tribal realm is established, what is the desire of that tribal realm? It is to create a nation. What is the desire of that nation? It is to create a world. Then, what is the desire of that world? If it starts from the source, as a result, if God exists, it is to return to the fundamental God who governs this result. 

Therefore, God is the one who governs this universe. In other words, God is the center and subject of the universe. There cannot be an objective or resultant existence without that central and subjective being.

In the unification of countries, it is necessary to determine which will be the subject and which will be the object. If both try to be subjects, what will happen? For one country to unite, numerous nations or ethnicities must unite. There must be a subject and an objective element in that one country; otherwise, it cannot become one. This is the same for ethnicities. Ethnicities have such relationships, and families also have such relationships, which we cannot deny. When we look at individuals, individuals are also in such positions. 

Now, the issue here is... we must find a principle. How will we find that principle? We need to carefully examine this issue. It involves the relationships you have established, that is, the relationship between subject and object, completely separating the pluses and minuses based on the plus, and separating the minuses based on the minus, step by step, creating individual pluses and family pluses, and in relation to those, creating individual minuses and family minuses step by step. If we create one from this, it will become one world. The theory is simple. In this way, when the country of the subject and the country of the counterpart unite and go to God, it becomes a world of unity. This is what we have learned from the principles. 

From this perspective, there is no one who does not desire this. 

Where does one world start? Where is the starting point? It starts from me. Then what is the principle? Unity or oneness means becoming one from two or more. 

The concept of 'I'... of course, when we consider 'I', we think of it centered around 'I', but we can understand that the very concept of 'I' has a surrounding nature. In other words, when you look at yourself, you are 'I' among relatives, among nations, and among the world. You must understand this. Today, when we commonly say 'I', we often think it starts and ends with ourselves without that concept, but that is not the case. We must recognize that we exist in a world of relationships. 

So, I am not something that arose from myself. There is a cause here. There is a cause, and then there is a result. If I am not a result, I am in a process heading toward a result, or I am in a position that remains there, and that is 'I'. We must become aware of such an 'I'. 

When we assert 'I', we must recognize that I represent two people. That is, there is the person of the heart, and there is the body. Now, 'I' does not refer to a position where the heart and body are separated and fighting against each other. It is our human nature to want to assert ourselves from a place where the heart and body are united. 

Then, 'I' must not change. It must remain unchanged. If there is a purpose in this universe, can the purpose of the universe change? It cannot change. Therefore, what I must pursue is... I must discover that I can assert an eternal and unchanging self. If I do not find that, I cannot establish a principle. 

Nothing that changes can achieve unity. Even if it becomes united, it will eventually break apart. It will fall apart. Therefore, for humans to seek a unified world, they must grasp eternity from a subjective position. Otherwise, we can discover here that we cannot establish a principle. 

What is the more valuable existence for me? It is the heart. 

So, where will we find the unchanging 'I'? We must understand what is closest to the unchanging essence, focusing on the heart and body. Here, we cannot help but bring forth the heart. The original heart does not change. 

And in establishing a subject, do we want a changing subject or an unchanging subject? There is no question; our true desire is to have an unchanging subject. The better it is, the more it should not change. Humans understand this, which is why they treasure and value what does not change. We can conclude here that such things are all symbolic representations. 

Therefore, the heart can become the subject for me. Why? Because the heart is close to eternity and the unchanging position. Thus, what is the more valuable existence for me? It is the heart, and we can theoretically conclude this from this perspective without contradiction. 

You (writing on the board) to rise to a higher level, to ascend to another level, it is all like this. In this position, the plus...
It becomes. This is how it develops. Now, because you have a heart within yourselves, this heart is a plus. So can this plus become one with this in front of it? What is this? "It's a minus." What that means is, centered around your heart, you cannot be without a body. If the heart and body cannot become one, the body pulls me. If God is the subject of the universe, and I become a subject with a plus heart and call out "God!" that God will not listen. It must be united with the body. Only then, when I call out "God!" will He respond.

So, if you look in the Bible, it says to resolve all enmities. If you have enmity with the body, you must resolve it with the heart... If enmity is formed in this universe, you cannot progress. If you get caught, you cannot move forward. If there is truth, the universe will support, welcome, and praise that truth; it is not meant to pull it back. This is a natural principle, yet if there is enmity, it pulls back and prevents movement. It pulls back. Then, if the plus position is the central position and it pulls back, what happens to the center? It disappears.

When you see this, you must understand that the command to forgive and love your enemies is not for the sake of the enemy, but for the sake of "me." And if the heart and body cannot become one, what happens? The body pulls me, it pulls me.

Do you want a unified world? "Yes." Where does it have to start from? "From myself." So how should it be done? It must be done according to this principle. It is simple. It is simple.

Until now, throughout human history, we have looked for everything through religion, cultivation, and so on, but we have not solved this one problem, yet we have claimed it is about cultivation or character.

Now, should we have desires or not? Should we have greed or not? "We should have them." Humans must have desires, but desires that follow the principle are what God desires; everyone desires that. What is the good desire that can make everything good? That is the principle of unity.

The reason men and women are in opposition is to automatically bring them together. Now, we must understand the principle of how to make "me" here. If we are men, this is the path a man should take... (pointing while writing) This is a man. And this is a woman. The woman is in opposition, in position. This is a woman. This is a minus. So, let's see. What is different between the character of a woman and the character of a man? A woman wants a masculine person, a masculine person. And a man wants a feminine person. They are originally different. Now, is there anyone who wants a woman like a man? A woman like a man? Do you want a man like a woman? (laughter) Small hands, no hair, looking like a woman. They are all in opposition, in relation.

Why is that? It is because it is meant to automatically bring them together. When you see this, (pointing to what was written) this is one inside and outside. If this happens, because of the woman and man, this character wants this and this character wants that, they become one. In other words, this is plus and minus, so they can become one. This and this... (laughter)

What does that mean? (pointing while writing) When this becomes one, these two combined are stronger than this, right? They are stronger than this and stronger than this. The plus and minus that have become one are stronger than the plus itself and stronger than the minus itself. Do you understand? "Yes." So this is strong. It becomes strong, and from here, it causes a plus action, a subjective action like God. Therefore, this becomes the subject. When these two combine, they become the subject, and since they have become the subject, from here... This is also in relation, so it can combine with this again. Thus, the whole can combine and become one subject. It is the same principle, the same.

If God is the perfect center of the universe, this is minus and this is plus. God is also a being like this. There is plus and minus. It is the same. Here, when this minus and plus combine, it becomes greater, so this keeps becoming one. Therefore, the statement that we can unify God is the same statement. Do you understand this principle? "Yes."

There is a secret to expelling Satan and unifying through serving others. Now, when your heart and body cannot completely become one, we must think about how to resolve that. Is that an easy thing? Then what will you do? We must think about how to make the heart and body one when they cannot become one. Think about that. Since it is difficult to make my heart and body one, if there is another person's plus and minus here, to make my minus one, the only conclusion is that I must stand in a position to serve others. That is the fastest way.

Once this starts to become one, it will gradually draw in. Therefore, if we follow the principles that religion advocates, it will be correct. That is why the statement to sacrifice and serve for others comes from here. Why? Because one cannot do it alone. If I make ten people good, if I give for the whole, those ten people become one with me. The act of Jesus tying a towel and washing the feet of the twelve disciples was to teach them to practice this principle.

Now, when we consider whether the path of making one through others is faster or the path of becoming one centered on myself is faster, the path of becoming one through myself is extremely difficult. Satan always occupies my body. But why must Satan retreat when I serve others? You must understand this problem. It is because that is the principle of the universe. When you go beyond for others, you enter a position that is better than Satan. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Satan serves himself. He serves himself. It is different.

In other words, when it comes to beating the Satan of my body, it is hard for me alone, but if I come out with the principle of serving others, because the principle of the universe, the principle of creation is such, Satan, who should serve God, cannot stand in a position to serve God and can step on and overcome the position where he stands to serve himself. Therefore, you must understand that there is a secret to expelling Satan through serving others.

Now, you can discover what the secret of unification is here. This law applies anywhere in the universe. It is a formula. A formula can apply anywhere in the universe, no matter how small. That is a formula.

In my personal life, if I do that, I can expel Satan; if I do that in my family, I can expel Satan; if I do that in my tribe, I can expel Satan; if I do that in my nation, I can expel the nation's Satan; if I do that in the world, I can expel the world's Satan; if I do that in the universe, I can expel the universe's Satan. Do you think so? "Yes."

Now, let's check that. If you genuinely care for one of your friends, does that friend follow you or not? Yes, if a person who serves themselves stays still, if you do not go, then they will follow. This is how it works.

Therefore, who becomes the subject? The one who is served or the one who serves? Who says "Thank you"? "Thank you"? The one who is served bows their head. The one who is served does that. Isn't that right? What that means is, "You are the subject, and I am the object." When you elect a village leader, you support such a person. You do not support someone who serves themselves; you support someone who serves the whole.

You must understand that there is a risk that a great Satan can arise in front of the Unification Church if we are not careful. Many people think, "The first person to enter the Unification Church is Abel, and the last person is Cain." That is wrong. If you live for the sake of entering the Unification Church, if you have lived for the sake of others until now, that person is undoubtedly Abel. A person who has moved and lived for themselves saying, "Oh, I entered first..." Not at all! That will not do. Do you understand Cain and Abel? "Yes."

Also, when the teacher appoints a regional director or a state representative, or when appointing a mobilization leader, one should not say, "Oh, I am Abel!" That is not how it works. "Serve me, serve me!" Is someone like that Abel? No, that is not the case. If you understand this principle, you must serve. You must serve and make it possible for others to serve automatically; that is what a responsible person should understand. Those who are currently receiving the 100-day training, who will go out to the regions and become pioneers or take on some central mission, must not get caught in this perspective.

Then, how can we know whether the Unification Church is a good church or a bad church? We can know this through this formula. It is wrong to say that we work for the Unification Church; it is wrong. We work for the nation.

If a nation believes in the Unification Church and it becomes the national religion, then that nation should say, "Our nation was established not for the Unification Church ideology for our nation, but for the Unification Church ideology for the world." That is how it should be.

Through this principle... To rise from the individual to the family, there must be a connection of all these processes, and this process must rise officially. It must be official. The world must rise through this formula.

If you want to live for the unification of the world or for the unification of your individual self, when I ask you, you will answer, "Ah, I want to live for the world." There are many desires. Then what should be done? It must be established that I do not live for my family, I do not live for my nation, I live for the world. That statement must be firmly established. So, do you want to live like that? "Yes." Then, to live for the world, even if you cannot...

The twelve disciples established by Jesus are representatives of the world nations. Americans say they do not like the number 13, right? I like it. I like it. (laughter) If you look at it centered around the twelve, you will understand, centered around the twelve. This is twelve. (pointing while writing) One, two, three... eleven, twelve, and the central number is taken as thirteen. It is not a straight line. This is not it. Do you dislike this? "No, I like it." This is the principle. This is the principle. These are all for the sake of others; these must all become one. This is the ideal. This is the purpose.

That is why Jesus told the disciples to "do this, do that" to make them one; did Jesus do it first? Which one is it? "Jesus did it first..." Why? Because it must align with the principles of the universe. So, through that play, after this becomes one, it goes this way.

By doing this, there is development in the universe. This must become one to develop. If it cannot become one, everything will fall apart. That is why when Jesus died on the cross, everything fell apart. Therefore, we must go this way and make all of this one. This can be said in terms of seasons, east, west, south, and north, as twelve all around, January, February, March, and the four seasons. The four seasons have become this way. So for a year to happen, the twelve months must become one. This is inseparable. Everything is inseparable. In the Bible, it says there are twelve pearl gates, right? Heaven is entered through these twelve pearl gates.

Therefore, if we make only twelve nations centered around world Christianity one, the world will automatically become one. If only three nations become one, that is where it starts. If only three nations become one, the twelve nations will begin to unite. That is why we must find three disciples. Our Unification Church should follow this principle.

In the time of Jesus, he tried to make twelve disciples centered around one nation, but in the ideal age to come, we must flatten the living standards that can establish representatives of twelve nations. In this way, when the representatives of the twelve nations centered around Jesus become one, the world will become one. That is certain.

Earlier, you said you would strive to create one world, but let’s think about how to create one world. The question here is whether you can live for the people of the twelve nations. (pointing while writing) The conclusion is that anyone who can dedicate their life to sacrifice for the twelve people, for the people of the twelve nations, can stand as a subject of the principled standard in creating this world. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

One world is achieved when we transcend nations and races and live for one another. Here in America, looking at the American people... If you observe America, the American people are a mixed ethnicity. It is a place where people from more than twelve nations gather. More than 120 countries' people are gathered here. If those people live for one another, then this nation is a nation of ideals. Where can you find a nation that hopes for more than that as humans? There is no nation that hopes for more than that. Is it like that here? "No." What about the black and white issues, the Jews are separate... They are all divided and scattered like this.

Therefore, if the citizens of this country all have our unification thought and decide to live like that, knowing that it is not just a matter of a short life but also an eternal world, then they cannot help but do it.

Do you want to do that? "Yes." You understand that, but do you really want to do it? "Yes." Then how can I know whether I am qualified to do that or not? It is simple. If the young men can say, "I am okay with any good girl from the twelve nations, whether she is from a developed country, an Asian, a white person, or a black person," then they can pass. They can always go beyond when looking for a partner. Then it is simple. The same goes for women. They should think, "To love the world, any man from any country is fine." (The following words are not recorded and cannot be included.) *
